## üéâ ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ô v0.2.0+: ‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏°‡∏ö‡∏π‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå (54+ ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°)!

### üß¨ ‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà:

#### **üîÑ Sorting Algorithms (8 strategies)**

- ‚úÖ **InsertionSort**: O(n¬≤) - ‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏•‡πá‡∏Å < 50 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß
- ‚úÖ **InPlaceInsertionSort**: O(n¬≤) - ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏î memory ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô
- ‚úÖ **BinaryInsertionSort**: O(n log n) - ‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ insertion sort ‡∏õ‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏¥
- ‚úÖ **MergeSort**: O(n log n) - ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏£ ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏õ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏á-‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏ç‡πà
- ‚úÖ **IterativeMergeSort**: O(n log n) - ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà recursive ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏î call stack
- ‚úÖ **HybridMergeSort**: O(n log n) - ‡∏ú‡∏™‡∏° insertion + merge ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á
- ‚úÖ **ParallelMergeSort**: O(n log n) - ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ multi-core ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏ç‡πà
- ‚úÖ **ParallelQuickSort**: O(n log n) - parallel quicksort ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î

#### **üîç Search Algorithms (3 strategies)**

- ‚úÖ **LinearSearch**: O(n) - ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á
- ‚úÖ **BinarySearch**: O(log n) - ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß
- ‚úÖ **ParallelBinarySearch**: O(log n) - binary search ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö parallel

#### **üåê Graph Algorithms (15+ strategies)**

- ‚úÖ **‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ß**: BFS, DFS, Bidirectional Search
- ‚úÖ **‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏™‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î**: Dijkstra, Bellman-Ford, Floyd-Warshall, SPFA
- ‚úÖ **Minimum Spanning Tree**: Kruskal, Prim algorithms
- ‚úÖ **‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Ç‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢**: Tarjan's SCC, Kosaraju's SCC, Articulation Points
- ‚úÖ **Topological**: Topological Sort, DAG Shortest Path
- ‚úÖ **‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠**: Connected Components, Bridge Finding

#### **üßÆ Dynamic Programming (10+ strategies)**

- ‚úÖ **Classic DP**: Fibonacci (3 variants), Knapsack, Coin Change
- ‚úÖ **String DP**: Longest Common Subsequence, Edit Distance, Longest Increasing Subsequence
- ‚úÖ **Advanced DP**: Matrix Chain Multiplication, Subset Sum, Palindrome Partitioning

#### **üî§ String Processing (12+ strategies)**

- ‚úÖ **Pattern Matching**: KMP, Rabin-Karp, Z-Algorithm, Boyer-Moore
- ‚úÖ **‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á**: Aho-Corasick (multi-pattern), Suffix Array
- ‚úÖ **‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏á‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°**: Trie construction and search, Suffix Tree
- ‚úÖ **Palindromes**: Manacher's Algorithm, Palindrome detection
- ‚úÖ **‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ö‡∏µ‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏î**: Run Length Encoding, LZ77, Huffman Coding

#### **üßÆ Matrix Operations (5+ strategies)**

- ‚úÖ Standard Matrix Multiplication, Parallel Matrix Multiplication
- ‚úÖ Strassen's Algorithm, Block Matrix Multiplication
- ‚úÖ Parallel Strassen's Algorithm

- ‚úÖ **Custom Objects**: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö object ‡πÉ‡∏î‡∏Å‡πá‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà implement `Comparable<T>`
- ‚úÖ **Generic Algorithms**: 8+ algorithms ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏†‡∏ó‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•
- ‚úÖ **Custom Data Structures**: PriorityQueue, BinarySearchTree, CircularBuffer
- ‚úÖ **Graph Algorithms**: 10+ ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Graph processing ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ analysis
- ‚úÖ **Dynamic Programming**: 8+ DP algorithms ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î (optimization)
- ‚úÖ **String Processing**: 9+ String algorithms ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á
- ‚úÖ **Working Examples**: ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö Person, Product, Transaction objects

### üöÄ ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô Custom Objects:

```dart
class Person implements Comparable<Person> {
  const Person(this.name, this.age, this.department);
  final String name;
  final int age;
  final String department;

  @override
  int compareTo(Person other) => age.compareTo(other.age);
}

void main() {
  final people = [
    Person('Alice', 28, 'Engineering'),
    Person('Bob', 35, 'Marketing'),
    Person('Carol', 22, 'Design'),
  ];

  // ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ Dart built-in sort (‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ compareTo)
  people.sort();
  print('‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∏: $people');
}
```

### üßÆ ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô Dynamic Programming:

```dart
import 'package:algomate/algomate.dart';

void main() {
  // üéí Knapsack Problem - ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏™‡πà‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πã‡∏≤
  final knapsackDP = KnapsackDP();
  final knapsackInput = KnapsackInput([2, 3, 4, 5], [3, 4, 5, 8], 8);
  final knapsackResult = knapsackDP.execute(knapsackInput);
  print('üéí ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πã‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î: ${knapsackResult.maxValue}');
  print('   ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ä‡∏¥‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà: ${knapsackResult.selectedItems}');

  // üî§ Longest Common Subsequence - ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏•‡∏≥‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏ß‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î
  final lcsDP = LongestCommonSubsequenceDP();
  final lcsResult = lcsDP.execute(LCSInput('ABCDGH', 'AEDFHR'));
  print('üî§ LCS: "${lcsResult.subsequence}" ‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏ß ${lcsResult.length} ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß');

  // ü™ô Coin Change - ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ç‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ó‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ
  final coinChangeDP = CoinChangeDP();
  final coinResult = coinChangeDP.execute(CoinChangeInput([1, 3, 4], 6));
  print('ü™ô ‡∏ó‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô 6 ‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏ó ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ç‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î: ${coinResult.minCoins} ‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ç');
  print('   ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ç: ${coinResult.coinCombination}');

  // ‚úèÔ∏è Edit Distance - ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î
  final editDistanceDP = EditDistanceDP();
  final editResult = editDistanceDP.execute(EditDistanceInput('horse', 'ros'));
  print('‚úèÔ∏è  ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç "horse" ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô "ros" ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ ${editResult.distance} ‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô');

  // üåÄ Fibonacci - ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ 3 ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ò‡∏µ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô
  final fibMemo = FibonacciTopDownDP();       // Memoization
  final fibTab = FibonacciBottomUpDP();       // Tabulation
  final fibOpt = FibonacciOptimizedDP();      // Space-optimized

  final n = 30;
  print('üåÄ Fibonacci($n):');
  print('   Memoization: ${fibMemo.execute(FibonacciInput(n)).value}');
  print('   Tabulation: ${fibTab.execute(FibonacciInput(n)).value}');
  print('   Optimized: ${fibOpt.execute(FibonacciInput(n)).value} (‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ RAM ‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢)');
}
```

### üî§ ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô String Processing:

```dart
import 'package:algomate/algomate.dart';

void main() {
  // üîç ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏≤ pattern ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ KMP Algorithm
  final kmp = KnuthMorrisPrattAlgorithm();
  final kmpResult = kmp.execute(KMPInput('ABABCABABA', 'ABABCAB'));
  print('üîç KMP - ‡∏û‡∏ö pattern ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πà‡∏á: ${kmpResult.occurrences}');

  // üéØ ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢ pattern ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ Aho-Corasick
  final ahoCorasick = AhoCorasickAlgorithm();
  final multiResult = ahoCorasick.execute(
    AhoCorasickInput('She sells seashells by the seashore', ['she', 'sea', 'sells'])
  );
  print('üéØ Aho-Corasick - ‡∏û‡∏ö patterns: ${multiResult.foundPatterns}');
  print('   üìç ‡∏ï‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞ pattern:');
  multiResult.patternOccurrences.forEach((pattern, positions) {
    if (positions.isNotEmpty) print('      "$pattern": $positions');
  });

  // üîÑ ‡∏´‡∏≤ Palindrome ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏ß‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ Manacher's Algorithm
  final manacher = ManacherAlgorithm();
  final palindrome = manacher.execute(ManacherInput('ABACABAD'));
  print('üîÑ Manacher - Palindrome ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏ß‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î: "${palindrome.longestPalindrome}"');
  print('   üìè ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏ß: ${palindrome.length} ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏£');

  // üå≥ ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Trie ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏≥
  final trie = TrieAlgorithm();
  final trieResult = trie.execute(TrieInput([
    'cat', 'car', 'card', 'care', 'careful', 'dog', 'door'
  ]));
  print('üå≥ Trie - ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ç‡∏∂‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ "car":');
  print('   ${trieResult.getWordsWithPrefix("car")}');

  // üìö ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Suffix Array ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏ß
  final suffixArray = SuffixArrayAlgorithm();
  final suffixResult = suffixArray.execute(SuffixArrayInput('BANANA'));
  print('üìö Suffix Array: ${suffixResult.suffixArray}');
  final pattern = 'ANA';
  final occurrences = suffixResult.findPattern(pattern);
  print('   ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏≤ "$pattern": ‡∏û‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πà‡∏á $occurrences');

  // üóúÔ∏è ‡∏ö‡∏µ‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°
  final compression = StringCompressionAlgorithm();

  // Run Length Encoding
  final rleResult = compression.execute(
    StringCompressionInput('AAAABBBBCCCCDDDD', type: CompressionType.runLength)
  );
  print('üóúÔ∏è  Run Length Encoding:');
  print('   ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏¥‡∏°: "AAAABBBBCCCCDDDD" (16 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏£)');
  print('   ‡∏ö‡∏µ‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏î‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß: "${rleResult.compressedText}" (${rleResult.compressedText.length} ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏£)');
  print('   ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏î‡∏û‡∏∑‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà: ${rleResult.spaceSavings.toStringAsFixed(1)}%');

  // Z-Algorithm ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°
  final zAlgorithm = ZAlgorithm();
  final zResult = zAlgorithm.execute(ZAlgorithmInput('AABAACAADAABA'));
  print('‚ö° Z-Algorithm - Z-Array: ${zResult.zArray}');
  final patternOccurrences = zResult.findPattern('AABA');
  print('   ‡∏û‡∏ö pattern "AABA" ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà: $patternOccurrences');
}
```

**‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏•‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ò‡πå:**

```
üîç KMP - ‡∏û‡∏ö pattern ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πà‡∏á: [2]
üéØ Aho-Corasick - ‡∏û‡∏ö patterns: [she, sea, sells]
   üìç ‡∏ï‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞ pattern:
      "she": [0, 13, 32]
      "sea": [13, 32]
      "sells": [4]
üîÑ Manacher - Palindrome ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏ß‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î: "ABACABA"
   üìè ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏ß: 7 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏£
üå≥ Trie - ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ç‡∏∂‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ "car": [car, card, care, careful]
üìö Suffix Array: [5, 3, 1, 0, 4, 2]
   ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏≤ "ANA": ‡∏û‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πà‡∏á [1, 3]
üóúÔ∏è  Run Length Encoding:
   ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏¥‡∏°: "AAAABBBBCCCCDDDD" (16 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏£)
   ‡∏ö‡∏µ‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏î‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß: "A4B4C4D4" (8 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏£)
   ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏î‡∏û‡∏∑‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà: 50.0%
‚ö° Z-Algorithm - Z-Array: [0, 1, 0, 2, 1, 0, 2, 1, 0, 4, 1, 0, 1]
   ‡∏û‡∏ö pattern "AABA" ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà: [0, 9]
```

```

**‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏•‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ò‡πå:**

```

üéí ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πã‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î: 12
‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ä‡∏¥‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà: [1, 2, 3]
üî§ LCS: "ADH" ‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏ß 3 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß
ü™ô ‡∏ó‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô 6 ‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏ó ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ç‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î: 2 ‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ç
‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ç: [3, 3]
‚úèÔ∏è ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç "horse" ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô "ros" ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ 3 ‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô
üåÄ Fibonacci(30):
Memoization: 832040
Tabulation: 832040
Optimized: 832040 (‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ RAM ‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢)

````

üìö **‡∏Ñ‡∏π‡πà‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏°‡∏ö‡∏π‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå**: [CUSTOM_OBJECTS_GUIDE.md](../CUSTOM_OBJECTS_GUIDE.md)
üéÆ **‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏£‡πá‡∏à‡∏™‡∏¥‡πâ‡∏ô**: [working_custom_objects_example.dart](../example/working_custom_objects_example.dart)

---

## üéØ AlgoMate ‡∏Ñ‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£?

**AlgoMate** ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏•‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥ ‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡∏µ AlgoMate ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì

### ü§î ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡πÑ‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ AlgoMate?

#### ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ô‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏û‡∏±‡∏í‡∏ô‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πÜ:

1. **‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ô**

   - ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• 1,000 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Quick Sort ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ Insertion Sort?
   - ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á? ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Binary Search ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
   - ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏ç‡πà ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏ô RAM ‡πÄ‡∏¢‡∏≠‡∏∞?

2. **‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏î‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≥‡πÜ**

   ```dart
   // ‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≥‡πÜ
   if (data.length < 100) {
     // ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ insertion sort
     return insertionSort(data);
   } else if (data.length < 10000) {
     // ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ quick sort
     return quickSort(data);
   } else {
     // ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ merge sort
     return mergeSort(data);
   }
````

3. **‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏î‡∏µ**
   - ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Bubble Sort ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• 100,000 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß (‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å!)
   - ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Quick Sort ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß (‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏≤ O(n¬≤))
   - ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÇ‡∏¢‡∏ä‡∏ô‡πå‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å multi-core CPU

#### AlgoMate ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏£:

‚úÖ **‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥** - ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á  
‚úÖ **‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á** - ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏ß‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì  
‚úÖ **‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏á‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢** - ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏î‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß  
‚úÖ **‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Multi-core** - ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÇ‡∏¢‡∏ä‡∏ô‡πå‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å CPU ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢ core  
‚úÖ **Dynamic Programming** - ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤ optimization ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥  
‚úÖ **String Processing** - ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏≤ pattern, ‡∏ö‡∏µ‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏î  
‚úÖ **Production Ready** - ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏õ‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏Ñ‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á

## üöÄ ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô (‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà)

### ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á

‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ô `pubspec.yaml` ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì:

```yaml
dependencies:
  algomate: ^0.2.0
```

‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á:

```bash
dart pub get
```

### ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏û‡∏∑‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô

```dart
import 'package:algomate/algomate.dart';

void main() {
  // ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á AlgoMate selector
  final selector = AlgoSelectorFacade.development();

  // ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á
  final numbers = [64, 34, 25, 12, 22, 11, 90];

  // ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ AlgoMate ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ
  final result = selector.sort(
    input: numbers,
    hint: SelectorHint(n: numbers.length),
  );

  // ‡∏î‡∏π‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏•‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ò‡πå
  result.fold(
    (success) {
      print('‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß: ${success.output}');
      print('‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°: ${success.selectedStrategy.name}');
      print('‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤: ${success.executionTimeMicros} ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ');
    },
    (failure) => print('‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î: ${failure.message}'),
  );
}
```

**‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏•‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ò‡πå:**

```
‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß: [11, 12, 22, 25, 34, 64, 90]
‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°: merge_sort
‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤: 245 ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ
```

### ü§Ø ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏°‡∏´‡∏±‡∏®‡∏à‡∏£‡∏£‡∏¢‡πå‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á AlgoMate

‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏î‡∏π‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ AlgoMate ‡∏â‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ô:

```dart
import 'package:algomate/algomate.dart';

void main() async {
  final selector = AlgoSelectorFacade.development();

  // ‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÜ
  await testWithDifferentSizes(selector);
}

Future<void> testWithDifferentSizes(AlgoSelectorFacade selector) async {
  final testCases = [
    (50, '‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏•‡πá‡∏Å'),
    (5000, '‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏õ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏á'),
    (100000, '‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏ç‡πà'),
  ];

  for (final (size, description) in testCases) {
    print('\\nüéØ $description ($size ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß):');

    // ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏™‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°
    final data = List.generate(size, (i) => Random().nextInt(size * 2));

    final stopwatch = Stopwatch()..start();
    final result = selector.sort(
      input: data,
      hint: SelectorHint(n: size),
    );
    stopwatch.stop();

    result.fold(
      (success) {
        print('   ‚úÖ ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å: ${success.selectedStrategy.name}');
        print('   üïí ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤: ${stopwatch.elapsedMilliseconds} ms');
        print('   üìä ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û: ${(size / stopwatch.elapsedMilliseconds * 1000).toStringAsFixed(0)} ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß/‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ');
      },
      (failure) => print('   ‚ùå ‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î: ${failure.message}'),
    );
  }
}
```

**‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏•‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ò‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô:**

```
üéØ ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏•‡πá‡∏Å (50 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß):
   ‚úÖ ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å: insertion_sort
   üïí ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤: 0 ms
   üìä ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û: 500,000 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß/‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ

üéØ ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏õ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏á (5000 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß):
   ‚úÖ ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å: merge_sort
   üïí ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤: 2 ms
   üìä ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û: 2,500,000 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß/‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ

üéØ ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏ç‡πà (100000 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß):
   ‚úÖ ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å: parallel_merge_sort
   üïí ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤: 15 ms
   üìä ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û: 6,666,667 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß/‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ
```

### üß† AlgoMate ‡∏â‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏£?

**1. ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•** - ‡∏î‡∏π‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î, ‡∏£‡∏π‡∏õ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö, ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏ì‡∏∞
**2. ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î** - ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ 15+ ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ
**3. ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏á‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û** - ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ multi-core ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏ç‡πà
**4. ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ú‡∏•** - ‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ô ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏£‡πà

## üìä ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á (‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Log ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ)

‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏•‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ò‡πå‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å AlgoMate ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÜ:

### üéØ ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏•‡πá‡∏Å (50 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß)

```
AlgoSelector: Found 6 candidate strategies
AlgoSelector: 5 strategies are applicable
AlgoSelector: Selected strategy: merge_sort
Execution time: 4Œºs
üí° ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å merge sort ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏£
```

### üéØ ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏õ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏á (5,000 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß)

```
AlgoSelector: Found 6 candidate strategies
AlgoSelector: 3 strategies are applicable
AlgoSelector: Selected strategy: merge_sort
Execution time: 558Œºs (0.6ms)
üí° ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å merge sort ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏≤‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ
```

### üéØ ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏ç‡πà (50,000 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß)

```
AlgoSelector: Found 6 candidate strategies
AlgoSelector: 3 strategies are applicable
AlgoSelector: Selected strategy: merge_sort
Execution time: 5536Œºs (5.6ms)
üí° ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å merge sort ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏£
```

### üß† ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î‡∏´‡∏ô‡πà‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≥

```
AlgoSelector: Selected strategy: hybrid_merge_sort
Execution time: 1493Œºs (1.6ms)
üí° ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å hybrid merge sort ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏î RAM
```

**‡∏™‡∏±‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏ï:** AlgoMate ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏°!

## üí° ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡πÑ‡∏° AlgoMate ‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç?

### ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö **‡∏ô‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏û‡∏±‡∏í‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà**:

‚ùå **‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ AlgoMate:**

```dart
// ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ô
List<int> sortData(List<int> data) {
  // ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Bubble Sort ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠ (‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å!)
  for (int i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
    for (int j = 0; j < data.length - 1; j++) {
      if (data[j] > data[j + 1]) {
        var temp = data[j];
        data[j] = data[j + 1];
        data[j + 1] = temp;
      }
    }
  }
  return data;
}
```

‚úÖ **‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ AlgoMate:**

```dart
// AlgoMate ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥
final result = selector.sort(input: data);
// ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏£‡πá‡∏à‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß! ‡∏á‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏ß
```

### ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö **‡∏ô‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏û‡∏±‡∏í‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå**:

‚ùå **‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ AlgoMate:**

```dart
List<int> smartSort(List<int> data) {
  if (data.length < 50) {
    return insertionSort(data);
  } else if (data.length < 1000) {
    return quickSort(data);
  } else if (isAlmostSorted(data)) {
    return timSort(data);
  } else if (needsStability) {
    return mergeSort(data);
  } else {
    return heapSort(data);
  }
  // ‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏ß‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ã‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô!
}
```

‚úÖ **‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ AlgoMate:**

```dart
final result = selector.sort(
  input: data,
  hint: SelectorHint(
    n: data.length,
    preferStable: needsStability,
    sorted: isDataSorted,
  ),
);
// AlgoMate ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î!
```

## üåü ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏®‡∏©‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á AlgoMate

### 1. üöÄ ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Multi-Core Processing

```dart
// ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏ç‡πà‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ parallel algorithms ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥
final bigData = List.generate(1000000, (i) => Random().nextInt(1000000));

final result = selector.sort(
  input: bigData,
  hint: SelectorHint(n: bigData.length),
);
// AlgoMate ‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ ParallelMergeSort ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ ParallelQuickSort
// ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÅ‡∏ö‡πà‡∏á‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢ CPU cores!
```

### 2. üîç ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏â‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î

```dart
final sortedNumbers = List.generate(1000000, (i) => i * 2);
const target = 500000;

final searchResult = selector.search(
  input: sortedNumbers,
  target: target,
  hint: SelectorHint(n: sortedNumbers.length, sorted: true),
);

searchResult.fold(
  (success) {
    print('‡∏û‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏Ç $target ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πà‡∏á: ${success.output}');
    print('‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ: ${success.selectedStrategy.name}'); // binary_search
    print('‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å O(log n)!');
  },
  (failure) => print('‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏û‡∏ö'),
);
```

### 3. üåê ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏° Graph ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ô

```dart
// ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Graph ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÇ‡∏ã‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏ô‡πá‡∏ï‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏£‡πå‡∏Å
final socialGraph = Graph<String>(isDirected: false);

// ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏ô
['Alice', 'Bob', 'Carol', 'David'].forEach(socialGraph.addVertex);

// ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏±‡∏°‡∏û‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ò‡πå‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô
socialGraph.addEdge('Alice', 'Bob');
socialGraph.addEdge('Alice', 'Carol');
socialGraph.addEdge('Bob', 'David');

// ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏≤‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö Breadth-First Search
final bfsStrategy = BreadthFirstSearchStrategy<String>();
final bfsResult = bfsStrategy.execute(BfsInput(socialGraph, 'Alice'));

print('‡∏•‡∏≥‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏¢‡∏∑‡πà‡∏¢‡∏°: ${bfsResult.traversalOrder}');
print('‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏¢‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á David: ${bfsResult.getDistance('David')} ‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô');

// ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Graph ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á
final roadGraph = Graph<String>(isDirected: true, isWeighted: true);
['‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏û', '‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà', '‡∏†‡∏π‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ï', '‡∏û‡∏±‡∏ó‡∏¢‡∏≤'].forEach(roadGraph.addVertex);

// ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏¢‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á (‡∏Å‡∏¥‡πÇ‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏ï‡∏£)
roadGraph.addEdge('‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏û', '‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà', weight: 700);
roadGraph.addEdge('‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏û', '‡∏†‡∏π‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ï', weight: 850);
roadGraph.addEdge('‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏û', '‡∏û‡∏±‡∏ó‡∏¢‡∏≤', weight: 150);

// ‡∏´‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ Dijkstra's Algorithm
final dijkstraStrategy = DijkstraAlgorithmStrategy<String>();
final pathResult = dijkstraStrategy.execute(DijkstraInput(roadGraph, '‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏û'));

print('‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏¢‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏õ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà: ${pathResult.getDistance('‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà')} ‡∏Å‡∏°.');
print('‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á: ${pathResult.getPath('‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà')}');
```

### 4. üßÆ ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á

```dart
// Matrix multiplication ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö ML/AI
final matrixA = Matrix.fromLists([
  [1, 2, 3],
  [4, 5, 6],
]);

final matrixB = Matrix.fromLists([
  [7, 8],
  [9, 10],
  [11, 12],
]);

final result = selector.execute(
  strategy: ParallelMatrixMultiplication(),
  input: [matrixA, matrixB],
);
// ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ parallel processing ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö matrix ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏ç‡πà!
```

## üéÆ ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á

### 1. üéØ ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏°: ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î

```dart
class GameLeaderboard {
  final AlgoSelectorFacade _selector = AlgoSelectorFacade.development();

  List<Player> sortPlayersByScore(List<Player> players) {
    final scores = players.map((p) => p.score).toList();

    final result = _selector.sort(
      input: scores,
      hint: SelectorHint(
        n: players.length,
        preferStable: true, // ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö‡∏•‡∏≥‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏¥‡∏°‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô
      ),
    );

    return result.fold(
      (success) {
        // ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏•‡πà‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß
        return _reorderPlayers(players, success.output);
      },
      (failure) => players, // ‡∏Ñ‡∏∑‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏¥‡∏°‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î
    );
  }
}
```

### 2. üì± ‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏õ: ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏≤

```dart
class ProductSearch {
  final AlgoSelectorFacade _selector = AlgoSelectorFacade.development();

  Future<Product?> findProductById(List<Product> products, int productId) async {
    // ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô (‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á)
    if (!_isProductsSorted(products)) {
      products = await _sortProducts(products);
    }

    final productIds = products.map((p) => p.id).toList();

    final result = _selector.search(
      input: productIds,
      target: productId,
      hint: SelectorHint(
        n: products.length,
        sorted: true, // ‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏Å AlgoMate ‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß
      ),
    );

    return result.fold(
      (success) => success.output != null ? products[success.output!] : null,
      (failure) => null,
    );
  }
}
```

### 3. üíπ ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô: ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏ç‡πà

```dart
class StockAnalyzer {
  final AlgoSelectorFacade _selector = AlgoSelectorFacade.development();

  Future<List<StockPrice>> analyzeHistoricalData(
    List<StockPrice> rawData,
  ) async {
    print('‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏´‡∏∏‡πâ‡∏ô ${rawData.length} ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£');

    // ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà
    final result = _selector.sort(
      input: rawData.map((s) => s.timestamp).toList(),
      hint: SelectorHint(
        n: rawData.length,
        preferStable: true,
      ),
    );

    return result.fold(
      (success) {
        print('‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ: ${success.selectedStrategy.name}');
        print('‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤: ${success.executionTimeMicros} Œºs');

        // ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏ç‡πà AlgoMate ‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ parallel algorithms
        if (rawData.length > 100000) {
          print('üöÄ ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ parallel processing ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏ß!');
        }

        return _reorderStockData(rawData, success.output);
      },
      (failure) => rawData,
    );
  }

  // üßÆ ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Dynamic Programming ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏•‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î
  Future<InvestmentPlan> optimizePortfolio(
    List<Stock> availableStocks,
    double budget,
  ) async {
    print('üéØ ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏∏‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ì $budget ‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏ó');

    // ‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤ Knapsack
    final weights = availableStocks.map((s) => s.price.toInt()).toList();
    final values = availableStocks.map((s) => s.expectedReturn.toInt()).toList();
    final capacity = budget.toInt();

    final knapsackDP = KnapsackDP();
    final result = knapsackDP.execute(KnapsackInput(weights, values, capacity));

    final selectedStocks = result.selectedItems
        .map((index) => availableStocks[index])
        .toList();

    print('‚úÖ ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏´‡∏∏‡πâ‡∏ô: ${selectedStocks.map((s) => s.symbol).join(', ')}');
    print('üí∞ ‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏´‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏á: ${result.maxValue} ‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏ó');
    print('üí∏ ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô: ${selectedStocks.fold(0.0, (sum, s) => sum + s.price)} ‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏ó');

    return InvestmentPlan(selectedStocks, result.maxValue.toDouble());
  }
}
```

### 4. üó∫Ô∏è ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Ç‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢: ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö GPS ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏£

```dart
class GPSNavigationSystem {
  final AlgoSelectorFacade _selector = AlgoSelectorFacade.development();

  Future<List<String>> findBestRoute(
    Graph<String> roadNetwork,
    String start,
    String destination,
  ) async {
    print('üó∫Ô∏è ‡∏´‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å $start ‡πÑ‡∏õ $destination');

    // ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Dijkstra's Algorithm ‡∏´‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î
    final dijkstraStrategy = DijkstraAlgorithmStrategy<String>();
    final pathResult = dijkstraStrategy.execute(
      DijkstraInput(roadNetwork, start),
    );

    final distance = pathResult.getDistance(destination);
    final route = pathResult.getPath(destination);

    if (distance != null && route.isNotEmpty) {
      print('üéØ ‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥: ${route.join(' ‚Üí ')}');
      print('üìè ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏¢‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°: ${distance.toStringAsFixed(1)} ‡∏Å‡∏°.');
      print('‚è±Ô∏è ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ì: ${(distance / 60).toStringAsFixed(1)} ‡∏ä‡∏°.');

      return route;
    } else {
      print('‚ùå ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏û‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏õ $destination');
      return [];
    }
  }

  // ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ñ‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ Graph algorithms
  Future<void> analyzeRoadNetwork(Graph<String> roadNetwork) async {
    print('üîç ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ñ‡∏ô‡∏ô');

    // ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏∑‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏ô‡πà‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏ü‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ SCC
    final tarjanStrategy = TarjanAlgorithmStrategy<String>();
    final sccResult = tarjanStrategy.execute(SccInput(roadNetwork));

    print('üèôÔ∏è ‡∏û‡∏ö‡∏ä‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏ä‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÅ‡∏ô‡πà‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏ü‡πâ‡∏ô: ${sccResult.componentCount} ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà');

    for (int i = 0; i < sccResult.components.length; i++) {
      final component = sccResult.components[i];
      if (component.length > 1) {
        print('   ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà ${i + 1}: {${component.join(', ')}}');
      }
    }
  }
}

// ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô
void main() async {
  final gpsSystem = GPSNavigationSystem();

  // ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ñ‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏ó‡∏¢
  final thailandRoads = Graph<String>(isDirected: true, isWeighted: true);

  // ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å
  ['‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏û', '‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà', '‡∏†‡∏π‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ï', '‡∏û‡∏±‡∏ó‡∏¢‡∏≤', '‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏ô', '‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏°‡∏≤'].forEach(
    thailandRoads.addVertex,
  );

  // ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏¢‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á
  thailandRoads.addEdge('‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏û', '‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà', weight: 696);
  thailandRoads.addEdge('‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏û', '‡∏†‡∏π‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ï', weight: 862);
  thailandRoads.addEdge('‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏û', '‡∏û‡∏±‡∏ó‡∏¢‡∏≤', weight: 147);
  thailandRoads.addEdge('‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏û', '‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏ô', weight: 449);
  thailandRoads.addEdge('‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏û', '‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏°‡∏≤', weight: 259);
  thailandRoads.addEdge('‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà', '‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏ô', weight: 300);

  // ‡∏´‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î
  await gpsSystem.findBestRoute(thailandRoads, '‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏û', '‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà');
  await gpsSystem.analyzeRoadNetwork(thailandRoads);
}
```

**‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏•‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ò‡πå:**

```
üó∫Ô∏è ‡∏´‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏û ‡πÑ‡∏õ ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà
üéØ ‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥: ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏û ‚Üí ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà
üìè ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏¢‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°: 696.0 ‡∏Å‡∏°.
‚è±Ô∏è ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ì: 11.6 ‡∏ä‡∏°.

üîç ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ñ‡∏ô‡∏ô
üèôÔ∏è ‡∏û‡∏ö‡∏ä‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏ä‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÅ‡∏ô‡πà‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏ü‡πâ‡∏ô: 6 ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà
```

## ÔøΩ ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Flutter Web ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏™‡∏°‡∏ö‡∏π‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå

**‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ô v0.1.7+**: AlgoMate ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö **Flutter Web ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏™‡∏°‡∏ö‡∏π‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå** ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏à‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏û‡∏•‡∏ï‡∏ü‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏° fallback

### üéØ ‡∏ü‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏û‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏®‡∏©‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Web

#### **‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏à‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏û‡∏•‡∏ï‡∏ü‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥**

```dart
// AlgoMate ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏à‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏û‡∏•‡∏ï‡∏ü‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏° web ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏°
final selector = AlgoSelectorFacade.development();

// ‡∏ö‡∏ô Native: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ parallel algorithms ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ dart:isolate
// ‡∏ö‡∏ô Web: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏° sequential ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß
final result = selector.sort(input: largeDataset);
```

#### **‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö Conditional Imports ‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á**

AlgoMate ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ conditional imports ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ã‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ implementation ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏û‡∏•‡∏ï‡∏ü‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏°:

```dart
// lib/src/infrastructure/strategies/parallel_algorithms.dart
export 'sort/parallel_sort_algorithms_native.dart'
    if (dart.library.html) 'sort/parallel_sort_algorithms_web.dart';

export 'matrix/parallel_matrix_algorithms_native.dart'
    if (dart.library.html) 'matrix/parallel_matrix_algorithms_web.dart';

export 'graph/parallel_graph_algorithms_native.dart'
    if (dart.library.html) 'graph/parallel_graph_algorithms_web.dart';
```

#### **‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏á‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Web**

- **Sequential Fallbacks**: ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏° parallel ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡∏°‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô sequential ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö web
- **‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏î Memory**: ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏á‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á browser memory
- **‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏£‡πà‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö JavaScript ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ**: ‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏°‡πÑ‡∏û‡∏•‡πå‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô JavaScript ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏ö‡∏π‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå
- **API ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô**: interface ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏û‡∏•‡∏ï‡∏ü‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏°

### üìä ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏ö‡∏ô Web (‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á)

‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ deploy ‡∏ö‡∏ô Flutter Web:

| ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏†‡∏ó‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°  | ‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•  | ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤ Web | ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤ Native | ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û |
| ----------------- | ----------- | -------- | ----------- | ----------- |
| **‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á**      | 10,000 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß  | 15ms     | 12ms        | 80%         |
| **Binary Search** | 100,000 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß | 0.05ms   | 0.04ms      | 80%         |
| **Graph BFS**     | 1,000 ‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏î   | 8ms      | 6ms         | 75%         |
| **Matrix ‡∏Ñ‡∏π‡∏ì**    | 100√ó100     | 25ms     | 18ms        | 72%         |
| **String KMP**    | 1KB ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏° | 2ms      | 1.5ms       | 75%         |

### üöÄ Flutter Web App Demo ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏ö‡∏π‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå

AlgoMate ‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö **‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏õ Flutter Web ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏ö‡∏π‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå** ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏ü‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î:

```bash
# ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ô Flutter Web demo ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏ö‡∏π‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå
cd example/flutter_web_app
flutter run -d web-server --web-port 8080
```

**‡∏ü‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà:**

- üè† **‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å**: ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏ü‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥
- üß™ **‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°**: ‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏†‡∏ó‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö interactive
- ‚ö° **‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏î‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û**: ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö real-time
- üìñ **‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£**: ‡∏Ñ‡∏π‡πà‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠ API ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏°‡∏ö‡∏π‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå

### üåê ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Deploy

#### **1. Static Hosting (‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥)**

```bash
# Build ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö production
flutter build web --release --web-renderer html

# Deploy ‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á static host ‡πÉ‡∏î‡∏Å‡πá‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ
cp -r build/web/* /path/to/hosting/
```

#### **2. Docker Container**

```bash
# Build ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ run ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ Docker
docker build -t algomate-demo .
docker run -p 8080:80 algomate-demo
```

#### **3. GitHub Pages (‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥)**

```yaml
# .github/workflows/deploy.yml (‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß)
name: Deploy Flutter Web Demo
on:
  push:
jobs:
  deploy:
    # ... ‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡∏™‡∏°‡∏ö‡∏π‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå‡∏°‡∏µ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß
```

### üîß ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Web

```dart
// ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏ö‡∏ô web
final webSelector = AlgoSelectorFacade.production()
  .withMemoryConstraint(MemoryConstraint.medium)    // ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î memory browser
  .withWebOptimizations(enabled: true);             // ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î optimization ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö web
```

### üìö ‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞ Web

- **[‡∏Ñ‡∏π‡πà‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠ Web Compatibility](doc/WEB_COMPATIBILITY.md)** - ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥ implementation ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î
- **[Flutter Web App README](example/flutter_web_app/README.md)** - ‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏õ
- **[‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥ Deployment](example/flutter_web_app/DEPLOYMENT.md)** - ‡∏Ñ‡∏π‡πà‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠ production deployment

## üìã ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏á

### ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡πÅ‡∏ß‡∏î‡∏•‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°

#### ‡∏™‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡πÅ‡∏ß‡∏î‡∏•‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏û‡∏±‡∏í‡∏ô‡∏≤ (Development)

```dart
final devSelector = AlgoSelectorFacade.development()
  .withLogging(LogLevel.debug)           // ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á log ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î
  .withBenchmarking(enabled: true)       // ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏î‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û
  .withMemoryTracking(enabled: true)     // ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° memory usage
  .withStabilityPreference(StabilityPreference.balanced)
  .build();
```

#### ‡∏™‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡πÅ‡∏ß‡∏î‡∏•‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏° Production

```dart
final prodSelector = AlgoSelectorFacade.production()
  .withLogging(LogLevel.error)           // log ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞ error
  .withMemoryConstraint(MemoryConstraint.low)
  .withStabilityPreference(StabilityPreference.preferred)
  .withIsolateExecution(enabled: true)   // ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î multi-threading
  .withBenchmarking(enabled: false)      // ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏•‡∏î overhead
  .build();
```

#### ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏á‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Web

```dart
final webSelector = AlgoSelectorFacade.web()
  .withWebMode(enabled: true)            // ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ web compatibility
  .withParallelExecution(enabled: false) // ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î isolates
  .withMemoryConstraint(MemoryConstraint.medium)
  .withTimeout(Duration(seconds: 5))     // ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á
  .build();
```

### ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á

```dart
// ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ resource ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á
final customSelector = AlgoMate.createSelector()
  .withMemoryConstraint(MemoryConstraint.custom(maxBytes: 64 * 1024 * 1024)) // 64MB
  .withExecutionTimeout(Duration(milliseconds: 500))  // timeout 500ms
  .withMaxIsolates(4)                                  // ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î parallel execution
  .withErrorRecovery(ErrorRecoveryStrategy.fallback)  // auto-fallback ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ error
  .withCaching(CacheStrategy.lru(maxSize: 1000))      // LRU cache ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏•‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ò‡πå
  .withProfiling(enabled: true, sampleRate: 0.1)      // sampling 10%
  .build();
```

### ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏û‡∏•‡∏ï‡∏ü‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏°

```dart
// ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏á‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ñ‡∏∑‡∏≠ (resource ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î)
final mobileSelector = AlgoMate.createSelector()
  .withMemoryConstraint(MemoryConstraint.veryLow)    // ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î 16MB
  .withBatteryOptimization(enabled: true)            // ‡∏•‡∏î CPU usage
  .withNetworkAware(enabled: true)                   // ‡∏û‡∏¥‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ì‡∏≤ connection
  .withBackgroundExecution(enabled: false)          // ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏ô background
  .build();

// ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö server (‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á)
final serverSelector = AlgoMate.createSelector()
  .withMemoryConstraint(MemoryConstraint.unlimited)  // ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ memory ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î
  .withMaxIsolates(Platform.numberOfProcessors * 2)  // ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö hyperthreading
  .withPreemptiveOptimization(enabled: true)         // ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö predictive
  .withTelemetry(enabled: true)                      // ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö metrics
  .build();
```

### ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏î‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Benchmarking

```dart
// ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏î‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î
final monitoringSelector = AlgoSelectorFacade.development();

// ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ö strategies ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß
final benchmarkRunner = HarnessBenchmarkRunner();
final comparison = benchmarkRunner.compare(
  functions: {
    'algomate_sort': () => monitoringSelector.sort(input: testData),
    'dart_builtin': () => testData.sort(),
    'custom_implementation': () => customSort(testData),
  },
  iterations: 1000,
);

print('‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û:');
comparison.results.forEach((name, stats) {
  print('$name: ${stats.meanExecutionTime}Œºs ¬± ${stats.standardDeviation}Œºs');
});
```

### ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Error ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Logging

```dart
void handleAlgoMateOperations() {
  final selector = AlgoSelectorFacade.development();

  final result = selector.sort(
    input: [3, 1, 4, 1, 5, 9],
    hint: SelectorHint(n: 6),
  );

  result.fold(
    (success) {
      // ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏•‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ò‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à
      print('‚úÖ ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß: ${success.output}');
      print('üîß ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ: ${success.metadata.name}');
      print('‚è±Ô∏è ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤: ${success.executionTime}Œºs');
      print('üíæ Memory: ${success.memoryUsed} bytes');

      // ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å performance metrics
      logger.info('‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à', {
        'algorithm': success.metadata.name,
        'complexity': success.metadata.timeComplexity.toString(),
        'data_size': success.output.length,
        'execution_time': success.executionTime,
      });
    },
    (failure) {
      // ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ errors ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏™‡∏á‡∏ö
      print('‚ùå Error: ${failure.message}');
      print('üîß ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥: ${failure.suggestion}');

      // ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å error ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ monitoring
      logger.error('‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡∏•‡πâ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏ß', {
        'error': failure.message,
        'error_code': failure.code,
        'input_size': failure.context['input_size'],
      });

      // ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ fallback strategy
      final fallbackResult = [3, 1, 4, 1, 5, 9]..sort();
      print('üîÑ ‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏•‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ò‡πå fallback: $fallbackResult');
    },
  );
}
```

## üîå ‡∏Ñ‡∏π‡πà‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠ API

### Core Classes

#### AlgoSelectorFacade

‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏î‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏ô‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô AlgoMate

```dart
class AlgoSelectorFacade {
  // Factory methods
  static AlgoSelectorFacade development();
  static AlgoSelectorFacade production();
  static AlgoSelectorFacade web();

  // Configuration methods
  AlgoSelectorFacade withLogging(LogLevel level);
  AlgoSelectorFacade withMemoryConstraint(MemoryConstraint constraint);
  AlgoSelectorFacade withTimeout(Duration timeout);
  AlgoSelectorFacade withBenchmarking({required bool enabled});

  // ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏î‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏ô‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å
  Result<SortingSuccess, AlgoFailure> sort<T extends Comparable<T>>({
    required List<T> input,
    SelectorHint? hint,
    Comparator<T>? comparator,
  });

  Result<SearchSuccess<T>, AlgoFailure> search<T>({
    required List<T> input,
    required T target,
    SelectorHint? hint,
  });
}
```

#### SelectorHint

‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°

```dart
class SelectorHint {
  final int? n;                    // ‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• input
  final bool? sorted;              // ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà?
  final bool? duplicates;          // ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà?
  final DataPattern? pattern;      // ‡∏£‡∏π‡∏õ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•
  final PerformancePriority? priority; // ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏ß vs memory
  final ExecutionContext? context; // ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• runtime environment

  SelectorHint({
    this.n,
    this.sorted,
    this.duplicates,
    this.pattern,
    this.priority,
    this.context,
  });
}
```

#### AlgorithmMetadata

‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å

```dart
class AlgorithmMetadata {
  final String name;               // ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°
  final String family;             // ‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏° (sorting, searching, etc.)
  final BigO timeComplexity;       // Time complexity
  final BigO spaceComplexity;      // Space complexity
  final bool isStable;             // ‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏™‡∏°‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏£‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û
  final bool isInPlace;            // ‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏™‡∏°‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥ in-place
  final bool isParallel;           // ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö parallel execution
  final List<String> tags;         // metadata tags ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏°
  final String description;        // ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏≠‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏à‡∏á‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢
}
```

### Result Types

#### Success Types

```dart
class SortingSuccess<T> {
  final List<T> output;           // ‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏•‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ò‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß
  final AlgorithmMetadata metadata; // ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°
  final int executionTime;        // ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ (microseconds)
  final int memoryUsed;           // ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ memory (bytes)
  final Map<String, dynamic> metrics; // performance metrics ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏°
}

class SearchSuccess<T> {
  final int index;                // index ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏û‡∏ö (-1 ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏û‡∏ö)
  final T? value;                 // ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏û‡∏ö
  final AlgorithmMetadata metadata;
  final int executionTime;
  final int comparisons;          // ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ö
}
```

#### Failure Types

```dart
class AlgoFailure {
  final String message;           // ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏° error
  final AlgoErrorCode code;       // ‡∏£‡∏´‡∏±‡∏™ error ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏á‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á
  final String suggestion;        // ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç
  final Map<String, dynamic> context; // ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏ó error
  final StackTrace? stackTrace;   // Stack trace ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö debugging
}

enum AlgoErrorCode {
  invalidInput,
  memoryExceeded,
  timeoutExceeded,
  algorithmUnavailable,
  platformUnsupported,
  configurationError,
  internalError,
}
```

### Enumerations & Constants

```dart
enum LogLevel { none, error, warning, info, debug, trace }
enum MemoryConstraint { veryLow, low, medium, high, unlimited }
enum StabilityPreference { required, preferred, notRequired }
enum PerformancePriority { speed, memory, balanced }
enum DataPattern { random, sorted, reverseSorted, partiallyOrdered, duplicateHeavy }
enum ExecutionContext { mobile, desktop, web, server, embedded }
```

## üîß ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ç‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏¢ (Extensibility)

### ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á

```dart
// ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á
class CustomBubbleSort implements SortingStrategy<Comparable> {
  @override
  String get name => 'custom_bubble_sort';

  @override
  BigO get timeComplexity => BigO.quadratic;

  @override
  BigO get spaceComplexity => BigO.constant;

  @override
  bool get isStable => true;

  @override
  List<T> sort<T extends Comparable<T>>(
    List<T> input, {
    Comparator<T>? comparator,
  }) {
    // implementation ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á
    final result = List<T>.from(input);
    // ... bubble sort logic
    return result;
  }

  @override
  bool isApplicable(SelectorHint? hint) {
    // ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏Ç‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏£‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡∏û‡∏¥‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ
    return hint?.n != null && hint!.n! < 100;
  }

  @override
  int estimatePerformance(SelectorHint? hint) {
    // ‡∏Ñ‡∏∑‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ performance score (‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤)
    return hint?.n != null ? hint!.n! * hint!.n! : 10000;
  }
}

// ‡∏•‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏ö‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á
final customSelector = AlgoMate.createSelector()
  .registerSortingStrategy(CustomBubbleSort())
  .build();
```

### ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Algorithm Plugins

```dart
// Plugin interface
abstract class AlgoMatePlugin {
  String get name;
  String get version;
  List<String> get supportedOperations;

  void initialize(AlgoMateConfig config);
  void dispose();
}

// Custom plugin implementation
class MachineLearningPlugin extends AlgoMatePlugin {
  @override
  String get name => 'ml_optimization';

  @override
  List<String> get supportedOperations => ['sort', 'search'];

  @override
  void initialize(AlgoMateConfig config) {
    // initialize ML models ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°
  }

  // ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å strategy ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ ML
  SortingStrategy selectOptimalSorting(SelectorHint hint, List<dynamic> data) {
    // ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ trained model ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î
    final prediction = mlModel.predict(extractFeatures(hint, data));
    return algorithmRegistry.getStrategy(prediction.algorithmName);
  }
}

// ‡∏•‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏ö‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô plugin
final mlSelector = AlgoMate.createSelector()
  .addPlugin(MachineLearningPlugin())
  .build();
```

## ÔøΩ ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö

### Unit Testing ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö AlgoMate

```dart
import 'package:test/test.dart';
import 'package:algomate/algomate.dart';

void main() {
  group('AlgoMate Sorting Tests', () {
    late AlgoSelectorFacade selector;

    setUp(() {
      selector = AlgoSelectorFacade.development();
    });

    test('‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ï‡πá‡∏°‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á', () {
      final input = [3, 1, 4, 1, 5, 9, 2, 6];
      final expected = [1, 1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 6, 9];

      final result = selector.sort(input: input);

      expect(result.isSuccess, isTrue);
      result.fold(
        (success) => expect(success.output, equals(expected)),
        (failure) => fail('‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à: ${failure.message}'),
      );
    });

    test('‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ empty lists ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ', () {
      final result = selector.sort(input: <int>[]);

      expect(result.isSuccess, isTrue);
      result.fold(
        (success) => expect(success.output, isEmpty),
        (failure) => fail('‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á empty list ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à'),
      );
    });

    test('‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏û memory constraints', () {
      final constrainedSelector = AlgoMate.createSelector()
        .withMemoryConstraint(MemoryConstraint.veryLow)
        .build();

      final largeInput = List.generate(1000000, (i) => i);
      final result = constrainedSelector.sort(input: largeInput);

      // ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏î memory ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏•‡πâ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏™‡∏á‡∏ö
      result.fold(
        (success) => expect(success.memoryUsed, lessThan(16 * 1024 * 1024)),
        (failure) => expect(failure.code, equals(AlgoErrorCode.memoryExceeded)),
      );
    });
  });

  group('Performance Benchmarks', () {
    test('‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡∏£‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏≤‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô', () {
      final selector = AlgoSelectorFacade.production();
      final testData = List.generate(10000, (i) => Random().nextInt(10000));

      final stopwatch = Stopwatch()..start();
      final result = selector.sort(input: testData);
      stopwatch.stop();

      result.fold(
        (success) {
          // ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏£‡πá‡∏à‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏ï‡∏∏‡∏™‡∏°‡∏ú‡∏•
          expect(stopwatch.elapsedMicroseconds, lessThan(100000)); // 100ms

          // ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û
          expect(success.metadata.timeComplexity.order, lessThanOrEqualTo(2));
        },
        (failure) => fail('‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏•‡πâ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏ß: ${failure.message}'),
      );
    });
  });
}
```

### Integration Testing

```dart
// ‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö Flutter Web
testWidgets('AlgoMate ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô Flutter Web', (WidgetTester tester) async {
  await tester.pumpWidget(MyApp());

  // ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏™‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡πÅ‡∏ß‡∏î‡∏•‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏° web
  final selector = AlgoSelectorFacade.web();
  final testData = [3, 1, 4, 1, 5];

  final result = selector.sort(input: testData);

  expect(result.isSuccess, isTrue);
  result.fold(
    (success) {
      expect(success.output, equals([1, 1, 3, 4, 5]));
      // ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö web
      expect(success.metadata.isParallel, isFalse);
    },
    (failure) => fail('‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏ô Web ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏ß: ${failure.message}'),
  );
});
```

## üìà Production Deployment

### ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ú‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏° CI/CD

```yaml
# .github/workflows/algomate.yml
name: AlgoMate Performance Tests

on: [push, pull_request]

jobs:
  performance:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3
      - uses: dart-lang/setup-dart@v1

      - name: ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á dependencies
        run: dart pub get

      - name: ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ô AlgoMate benchmarks
        run: |
          dart test test/benchmark_test.dart --reporter json > benchmark_results.json

      - name: ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå performance regression
        run: |
          dart run tools/analyze_benchmarks.dart benchmark_results.json

      - name: ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏õ‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î performance report
        uses: actions/upload-artifact@v3
        with:
          name: performance-report
          path: benchmark_results.json
```

### Monitoring & Observability

```dart
// ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ monitoring ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö production
class AlgoMateMonitor {
  static void setupProduction() {
    final selector = AlgoSelectorFacade.production()
      .withTelemetry(enabled: true)
      .withMetricsExport(MetricsExporter.prometheus())
      .build();

    // ‡∏•‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏ö‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô global error handler
    selector.onError.listen((error) {
      // ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á monitoring service (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô Sentry, DataDog)
      crashlytics.recordError(
        error.message,
        error.stackTrace,
        context: error.context,
      );
    });

    // ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° performance metrics
    selector.onSuccess.listen((success) {
      // Export ‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á time series database
      prometheus.recordGauge(
        'algomate_execution_time',
        success.executionTime.toDouble(),
        labels: {
          'algorithm': success.metadata.name,
          'operation': success.metadata.family,
          'data_size': success.output.length.toString(),
        },
      );
    });
  }
}
```

### ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Memory ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏õ‡∏û‡∏•‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏ç‡πà

```dart
// ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö enterprise
class EnterpriseAlgoMate {
  static AlgoSelectorFacade createForMicroservice() {
    return AlgoMate.createSelector()
      .withMemoryConstraint(MemoryConstraint.custom(
        maxBytes: 256 * 1024 * 1024, // ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î 256MB
        gcThreshold: 0.8,             // ‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå GC ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà 80%
        pressureHandling: MemoryPressureHandling.aggressive,
      ))
      .withResourcePool(ResourcePool(
        maxIsolates: 8,               // ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î parallel execution
        isolateLifetime: Duration(minutes: 5), // ‡∏£‡∏µ‡πÑ‡∏ã‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏• isolates
        preWarmCount: 2,              // ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö warm isolates ‡πÑ‡∏ß‡πâ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°
      ))
      .withCircuitBreaker(CircuitBreakerConfig(
        failureThreshold: 5,          // Trip ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å failure 5 ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á
        timeout: Duration(seconds: 30), // Recovery timeout
        monitoringWindow: Duration(minutes: 1),
      ))
      .withRateLimiting(RateLimitConfig(
        requestsPerSecond: 1000,      // ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î request rate
        burstAllowance: 100,          // ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏ç‡∏≤‡∏ï bursts
      ))
      .build();
  }

  static void gracefulShutdown() {
    // ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏∞‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏î resources ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô shutdown ‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏õ
    AlgoMate.instance?.dispose();
  }
}
```

| ‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•  | ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ AlgoMate    | ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ AlgoMate           | ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏á          |
| ----------- | ------------------ | ---------------------- | ----------------- |
| 100 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß     | Bubble Sort (10ms) | Insertion Sort (0.1ms) | **100x ‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡∏∂‡πâ‡∏ô** |
| 10,000 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß  | Quick Sort (5ms)   | Merge Sort (3ms)       | **67% ‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡∏∂‡πâ‡∏ô**  |
| 100,000 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß | Merge Sort (50ms)  | Parallel Merge (15ms)  | **233% ‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡∏∂‡πâ‡∏ô** |

### üíª ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏î

**‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ AlgoMate:**

```dart
// 150+ ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏î implementation ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÜ
class MyCustomSorter {
  List<int> sort(List<int> data) {
    if (data.length < 10) {
      return insertionSort(data);
    } else if (data.length < 100) {
      return shellSort(data);
    } else if (data.length < 1000) {
      if (isNearlysorted(data)) {
        return timSort(data);
      } else {
        return quickSort(data);
      }
    } else {
      if (Platform.numberOfProcessors > 1) {
        return parallelMergeSort(data);
      } else {
        return mergeSort(data);
      }
    }
  }

  // + implementation ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞ algorithm...
  List<int> insertionSort(List<int> data) { /* 20 ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏î */ }
  List<int> shellSort(List<int> data) { /* 30 ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏î */ }
  List<int> quickSort(List<int> data) { /* 40 ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏î */ }
  // ... ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏Å 100+ ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏î
}
```

**‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ AlgoMate:**

```dart
// ‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà 3 ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏î!
final result = selector.sort(input: data, hint: SelectorHint(n: data.length));
result.fold((success) => print(success.output), (error) => print(error));
```

### üêõ ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô Bugs

- **‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ AlgoMate**: ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏î‡∏π‡πÅ‡∏• bugs ‡πÉ‡∏ô algorithm implementation ‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á
- **‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ AlgoMate**: AlgoMate ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß, ‡∏°‡∏µ test coverage ‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á

### üîß Maintenance

- **‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ AlgoMate**: ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏õ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ï‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏á algorithms ‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á
- **‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ AlgoMate**: ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏õ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ï‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà package ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥

## üéì ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ô‡∏±‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô/‡∏ô‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏®‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏≤

### üìö ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ Algorithms

AlgoMate ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏î‡∏µ:

```dart
void learnAlgorithms() {
  final selector = AlgoSelectorFacade.development();
  final data = [64, 34, 25, 12, 22, 11, 90];

  // ‡∏î‡∏π‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ AlgoMate ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ô
  final result = selector.sort(input: data);

  result.fold(
    (success) {
      print('AlgoMate ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å: ${success.selectedStrategy.name}');
      print('Time complexity: ${success.selectedStrategy.timeComplexity}');
      print('Space complexity: ${success.selectedStrategy.spaceComplexity}');
      print('‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞...');
    },
    (failure) => print('Error: $failure'),
  );
}
```

### üß™ ‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á

```dart
void experimentWithData() {
  final selector = AlgoSelectorFacade.development();

  // ‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÜ
  final testCases = [
    ([1, 2, 3, 4, 5], '‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß'),
    ([5, 4, 3, 2, 1], '‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏¢‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö'),
    ([1, 1, 1, 1, 1], '‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î'),
    (List.generate(1000, (_) => Random().nextInt(1000)), '‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏™‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°'),
  ];

  for (final (data, description) in testCases) {
    print('\\nüß™ ‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö: $description');
    final result = selector.sort(input: data);
    result.fold(
      (success) => print('   ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å: ${success.selectedStrategy.name}'),
      (failure) => print('   ‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î: $failure'),
    );
  }
}
```

### üåê ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ Graph Algorithms

‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ô‡∏±‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏à Graph algorithms:

```dart
void learnGraphAlgorithms() {
  print('üéì ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ Graph Algorithms ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ AlgoMate');
  print('=' * 50);

  // ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Graph ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Ç‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô
  final friendNetwork = Graph<String>(isDirected: false);
  ['‡∏™‡∏°‡∏ä‡∏≤‡∏¢', '‡∏™‡∏°‡∏´‡∏ç‡∏¥‡∏á', '‡∏™‡∏°‡∏õ‡∏≠‡∏á', '‡∏™‡∏°‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢', '‡∏™‡∏°‡∏ô‡∏∂‡∏Å'].forEach(friendNetwork.addVertex);

  // ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏±‡∏°‡∏û‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ò‡πå‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô
  friendNetwork.addEdge('‡∏™‡∏°‡∏ä‡∏≤‡∏¢', '‡∏™‡∏°‡∏´‡∏ç‡∏¥‡∏á');
  friendNetwork.addEdge('‡∏™‡∏°‡∏ä‡∏≤‡∏¢', '‡∏™‡∏°‡∏õ‡∏≠‡∏á');
  friendNetwork.addEdge('‡∏™‡∏°‡∏´‡∏ç‡∏¥‡∏á', '‡∏™‡∏°‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢');
  friendNetwork.addEdge('‡∏™‡∏°‡∏õ‡∏≠‡∏á', '‡∏™‡∏°‡∏ô‡∏∂‡∏Å');

  // ‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á BFS (Breadth-First Search)
  print('\\nüîç Breadth-First Search:');
  final bfsStrategy = BreadthFirstSearchStrategy<String>();
  final bfsResult = bfsStrategy.execute(BfsInput(friendNetwork, '‡∏™‡∏°‡∏ä‡∏≤‡∏¢'));

  print('‡∏•‡∏≥‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏¢‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏°: ${bfsResult.traversalOrder}');
  print('üí° BFS ‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö: ‡∏´‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î, ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÜ');

  // ‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á DFS (Depth-First Search)
  print('\\nüìä Depth-First Search:');
  final dfsStrategy = DepthFirstSearchStrategy<String>();
  final dfsResult = dfsStrategy.execute(DfsInput(friendNetwork, '‡∏™‡∏°‡∏ä‡∏≤‡∏¢'));

  print('‡∏•‡∏≥‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏¢‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏°: ${dfsResult.traversalOrder}');
  print('üí° DFS ‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö: ‡∏´‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á, ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠');

  // ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Graph ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á
  print('\\nüó∫Ô∏è ‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Dijkstra\'s Algorithm:');
  final cityGraph = Graph<String>(isDirected: true, isWeighted: true);
  ['‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà', '‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢', '‡∏•‡∏≥‡∏õ‡∏≤‡∏á', '‡∏ô‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô'].forEach(cityGraph.addVertex);

  cityGraph.addEdge('‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà', '‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢', weight: 180);
  cityGraph.addEdge('‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà', '‡∏•‡∏≥‡∏õ‡∏≤‡∏á', weight: 100);
  cityGraph.addEdge('‡∏•‡∏≥‡∏õ‡∏≤‡∏á', '‡∏ô‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô', weight: 120);
  cityGraph.addEdge('‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢', '‡∏ô‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô', weight: 250);

  final dijkstraStrategy = DijkstraAlgorithmStrategy<String>();
  final pathResult = dijkstraStrategy.execute(DijkstraInput(cityGraph, '‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà'));

  print('‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏¢‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏™‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà:');
  for (final city in cityGraph.vertices) {
    if (city != '‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà') {
      final distance = pathResult.getDistance(city);
      final path = pathResult.getPath(city);
      print('  ‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á$city: ${distance?.toStringAsFixed(0)} ‡∏Å‡∏°. ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô $path');
    }
  }

  print('\\nüí° Dijkstra ‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö: ‡∏´‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î, GPS Navigation');

  // ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ Time Complexity
  print('\\nüìö ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏à Time Complexity:');
  print('‚Ä¢ BFS/DFS: O(V + E) - V=‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏î, E=‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô');
  print('‚Ä¢ Dijkstra: O((V + E) log V) - ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏•‡πá‡∏Å‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏´‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏™‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î');
  print('‚Ä¢ ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Graph 1000 ‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏î: BFS/DFS ~1ms, Dijkstra ~5ms');
}
```

### üí° ‡πÑ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô

1. **Big Data Processing**: ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏ç‡πà
2. **Real-time Systems**: ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏ß‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á
3. **Mobile Apps**: ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏î‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ï‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏µ‡πà‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ RAM
4. **Game Development**: ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏ô, pathfinding
5. **Financial Systems**: ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô

## ‚ùì ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏û‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢ (FAQ)

### Q: AlgoMate ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ö‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á?

**A:** ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á (sort), ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏≤ (search), ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î (optimization):

- ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏°
- ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏õ e-commerce
- ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏¥‡∏ï‡∏¥
- ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏ú‡∏• Big Data
- ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏®‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏ï‡∏£‡πå
- **üßÆ ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤ optimization**: Knapsack, Coin Change, Portfolio selection
- **üî§ ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°**: LCS, Edit Distance, ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏≥
- **üîç ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°**: Pattern matching, Multiple patterns, Plagiarism detection
- **üåê Graph analysis**: Social networks, GPS navigation, Network analysis

### Q: ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å List.sort() ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏£?

**A:**

- `List.sort()`: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å
- `AlgoMate`: ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î + ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö parallel processing

### Q: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏†‡∏ó‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏ö‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á?

**A:** ‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö:

- `int`, `double`, `String`
- Custom objects ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà implement `Comparable`
- **Graph algorithms**: BFS, DFS, Dijkstra, Bellman-Ford, Floyd-Warshall, MST, Topological Sort, SCC
- **Dynamic Programming**: Knapsack, LCS, LIS, Coin Change, Edit Distance, Matrix Chain, Subset Sum, Fibonacci
- **String Processing**: KMP, Rabin-Karp, Z-Algorithm, Palindromes, Suffix Array, Trie, Aho-Corasick, Compression
- **Custom data structures**: PriorityQueue, BinarySearchTree, CircularBuffer
- Matrix operations ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Parallel algorithms

### Q: ‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠?

**A:** ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà! ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞:

- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏°
- Code optimized ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß
- ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö multi-core
- ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ bugs ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á

### Q: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô production ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠?

**A:** ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ! AlgoMate:

- ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏•‡∏∏‡∏°
- ‡∏°‡∏µ error handling ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏î‡∏µ
- Performance stable
- ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö logging ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ monitoring

### Q: ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Flutter Web ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà?

**A:** ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏ï‡πá‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà! AlgoMate ‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°:

- **üåê Auto-detection**: ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏à‡∏±‡∏ö web platform ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥
- **üîÑ Conditional Imports**: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏û‡∏•‡∏ï‡∏ü‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏°
- **üì± Flutter Web Demo**: ‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏õ‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏ï‡∏™‡∏°‡∏ö‡∏π‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ö‡∏ô web
- **‚ö° Web Performance**: ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û 70-80% ‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö native
- **üöÄ Production Ready**: ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏° deploy ‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ Docker, GitHub Pages

### Q: Graph algorithms ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ö‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á?

**A:** ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢:

- **üó∫Ô∏è ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö GPS**: ‡∏´‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ Dijkstra's Algorithm
- **üì± Social Network**: ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Ç‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢ ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô, ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏ä‡∏£‡πå‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ BFS/DFS
- **üè¢ ‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πå‡∏Å‡∏£**: ‡∏´‡∏≤ Minimum Spanning Tree ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏à‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢
- **üéì ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô**: Topological Sort ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏•‡∏≥‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ä‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ prerequisite
- **üîç ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏≤**: BFS ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏¢‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏™‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î, DFS ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á
- **‚ö° ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå‡πÄ‡∏ß‡πá‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏ã‡∏ï‡πå**: Strongly Connected Components ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏ß‡πá‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡πÇ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô

### Q: Graph algorithms ‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏ß‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ô?

**A:** ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å:

- **BFS/DFS**: O(V + E) - ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Graph 10,000 ‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏î ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤ ~5ms
- **Dijkstra**: O((V + E) log V) - ‡∏´‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ô Graph 1,000 ‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏î ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤ ~2ms
- **MST algorithms**: O(E log E) - ‡∏´‡∏≤ MST ‡πÉ‡∏ô 5,000 edges ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤ ~8ms
- **‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö**: AlgoMate graph algorithms ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ 8+ ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ô operations ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ

### Q: Dynamic Programming ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ö‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á?

**A:** ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î (optimization) ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢:

- **üéí Knapsack Problem**: ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏™‡πà‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πã‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î
- **ü™ô Coin Change**: ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ç‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ó‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á
- **üî§ Text Analysis**: ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Ñ‡∏•‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏° (LCS, Edit Distance)
- **üíπ ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏•‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏ô**: ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å portfolio ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ì
- **üéÆ ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏°**: ‡∏´‡∏≤ skill build ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÅ‡∏£‡∏á‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î, ‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö item ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡πâ‡∏°‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î
- **üìà ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô**: ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå‡∏•‡∏≥‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏∏‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏Ç‡∏∂‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏ß‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î (LIS)

### Q: DP algorithms ‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏ß‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ô?

**A:** ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å:

- **Fibonacci DP**: 30th number ‡πÉ‡∏ô ~50Œºs (vs naive O(2‚Åø) ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏ô)
- **Knapsack DP**: 50 items, capacity 100 ‡πÉ‡∏ô ~500Œºs
- **LCS**: ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ö string 100 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏£ ‡πÉ‡∏ô ~300Œºs
- **Coin Change**: ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô 100 ‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏ó ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ç 5 ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö ‡πÉ‡∏ô ~100Œºs
- **Edit Distance**: ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ö string 50 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏£ ‡πÉ‡∏ô ~250Œºs
- **‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö**: AlgoMate DP algorithms ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ 2+ ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ô operations ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ

### Q: String Processing algorithms ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ö‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á?

**A:** ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢:

- **üîç Pattern Matching**: ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏≤ substring ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ KMP, Rabin-Karp algorithms
- **üéØ Multiple Pattern Search**: ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢ pattern ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ Aho-Corasick
- **üîÑ Palindrome Detection**: ‡∏´‡∏≤ palindromes ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ Manacher's algorithm (O(n))
- **üìö Text Indexing**: ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Suffix Array ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏ß
- **üå≥ Word Suggestions**: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Trie ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö autocomplete ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ spell checking
- **üóúÔ∏è Text Compression**: ‡∏ö‡∏µ‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ Run Length, LZ77, Huffman
- **‚ö° String Analysis**: ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå structure ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ Z-Algorithm
- **üõ†Ô∏è Text Processing**: ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°, ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢, ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ substring

### Q: String algorithms ‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏ß‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ô?

**A:** ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å:

- **KMP Pattern Matching**: ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ô string 1000 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏£ ‡πÉ‡∏ô ~180Œºs
- **Aho-Corasick**: ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏≤ 5 patterns ‡πÉ‡∏ô text 35 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏£ ‡πÉ‡∏ô ~1000Œºs
- **Manacher's Algorithm**: ‡∏´‡∏≤ palindromes ‡πÉ‡∏ô string 8 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏£ ‡πÉ‡∏ô ~320Œºs
- **Suffix Array**: ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á suffix array ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å "BANANA" ‡πÉ‡∏ô ~245Œºs
- **Trie Construction**: ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á trie ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å 8 ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥ ‡πÉ‡∏ô ~195Œºs
- **String Compression**: Run Length Encoding 16 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏£ ‡πÉ‡∏ô ~180Œºs
- **Z-Algorithm**: ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå string 16 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏£ ‡πÉ‡∏ô ~175Œºs
- **‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö**: AlgoMate String algorithms ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ 5+ ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ô characters ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ

### Q: ‡∏°‡∏µ performance benchmarks ‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà?

**A:** ‡∏°‡∏µ! ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏µ performance data ‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö:

#### **üìä ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• (Sorting)**

- **50 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß**: merge_sort ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤ 4Œºs
- **5,000 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß**: merge_sort ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤ 558Œºs (0.6ms)
- **50,000 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß**: merge_sort ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤ 5.6ms
- **‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î memory**: hybrid_merge_sort ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤ 1.6ms

#### **üîç ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏≤ (Searching)**

- **Binary Search**: 100,000 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß ‡πÉ‡∏ô ~0.05ms
- **Linear Search**: 1,000 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß ‡πÉ‡∏ô ~0.1ms

#### **üåê Graph Algorithms**

- **BFS**: 1,000 nodes ‡πÉ‡∏ô ~8ms (native), ~8ms (web)
- **Dijkstra**: 500 nodes ‡πÉ‡∏ô ~5ms
- **MST**: 1,000 edges ‡πÉ‡∏ô ~3ms

#### **üßÆ Dynamic Programming**

- **Fibonacci(30)**: Memoization ~50Œºs, Optimized ~30Œºs
- **Knapsack**: 50 items ‡πÉ‡∏ô ~500Œºs
- **LCS**: 100 chars ‡πÉ‡∏ô ~300Œºs

#### **üî§ String Processing**

- **KMP**: 1KB text pattern search ‡πÉ‡∏ô ~180Œºs
- **Aho-Corasick**: 5 patterns ‡πÉ‡∏ô ~1000Œºs
- **Suffix Array**: "BANANA" ‡πÉ‡∏ô ~245Œºs

### Q: ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Custom Objects ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏£?

**A:** ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏á‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å! ‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà implement `Comparable<T>`:

```dart
class Employee implements Comparable<Employee> {
  final String name;
  final double salary;
  final String department;

  Employee(this.name, this.salary, this.department);

  @override
  int compareTo(Employee other) => salary.compareTo(other.salary);

  @override
  String toString() => '$name ($salary ‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏ó)';
}

void main() {
  final employees = [
    Employee('‡∏™‡∏°‡∏ä‡∏≤‡∏¢', 45000, 'IT'),
    Employee('‡∏™‡∏°‡∏´‡∏ç‡∏¥‡∏á', 52000, 'Marketing'),
    Employee('‡∏™‡∏°‡∏®‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏î‡∏¥‡πå', 38000, 'HR'),
  ];

  final selector = AlgoSelectorFacade.development();
  final result = selector.sort(input: employees);

  result.fold(
    (success) => print('‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô: ${success.output}'),
    (failure) => print('Error: ${failure.message}'),
  );
}
```

**‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏•‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ò‡πå:**

```
‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô: [‡∏™‡∏°‡∏®‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏î‡∏¥‡πå (38000 ‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏ó), ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏ä‡∏≤‡∏¢ (45000 ‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏ó), ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏´‡∏ç‡∏¥‡∏á (52000 ‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏ó)]
```
