### Q: ‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏£?

**A:** ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô 3 ‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô:

#### **1. ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á**

```yaml
# pubspec.yaml
dependencies:
  algomate: ^0.1.7
```

#### **2. Import ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô**

```dart
import 'package:algomate/algomate.dart';

void main() {
  final selector = AlgoSelectorFacade.development();
  final data = [64, 34, 25, 12, 22, 11, 90];

  final result = selector.sort(input: data);
  result.fold(
    (success) => print('‚úÖ ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß: ${success.output}'),
    (failure) => print('‚ùå Error: ${failure.message}'),
  );
}
```

#### **3. ‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏•‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ò‡πå**

```
‚úÖ ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß: [11, 12, 22, 25, 34, 64, 90]
```

### Q: ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÇ‡∏õ‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏Ñ‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?

**A:** ‡∏°‡∏µ! ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á:

- **üì± Flutter Web Demo**: ‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏õ web ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏ö‡∏π‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á
- **üéÆ Game Leaderboard**: ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏°
- **üíπ Stock Analysis**: ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏´‡∏∏‡πâ‡∏ô
- **üó∫Ô∏è GPS Navigation**: ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á
- **üõí E-commerce Search**: ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏≤

‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ:

```bash
# Flutter Web App Demo
cd example/flutter_web_app
flutter run -d web-server --web-port 8080

# Command Line Examples
dart run example/complete_demo.dart
```

## ü§ù ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏£‡πà‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏û‡∏±‡∏í‡∏ô‡∏≤

### üåü ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ô

‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏ä‡∏≠‡∏ö AlgoMate ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏°:

- ‚≠ê **Star** ‡πÉ‡∏ô [GitHub](https://github.com/Kidpech-code/algomate)
- üëç **Like** ‡πÉ‡∏ô [pub.dev](https://pub.dev/packages/algomate)
- üìù **‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô Review**: ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡πà‡∏á‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô
- üó£Ô∏è **‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô**: ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ß‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏ú‡∏¢‡πÅ‡∏û‡∏£‡πà‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏ó‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏µ‡πÜ

### üêõ ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏ü‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå

‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏≠ bug ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏µ‡πÑ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î‡∏µ‡πÜ:

### üöÄ ‡∏£‡πà‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏û‡∏±‡∏í‡∏ô‡∏≤ (Contributing)

‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏û‡∏±‡∏í‡∏ô‡∏≤ AlgoMate:

#### **‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ô‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏û‡∏±‡∏í‡∏ô‡∏≤ Beginner**

1. üìñ **‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£**: ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ß‡∏¢‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏´‡∏≤ typos, ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á
2. üß™ **‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô Tests**: ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° test cases ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà
3. üîç **‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô Bugs**: ‡∏´‡∏≤ bugs ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ)

#### **‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ô‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏û‡∏±‡∏í‡∏ô‡∏≤ Intermediate**

1. üîß **‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ Bugs**: ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å issues ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢ "good first issue"
2. ‚ú® **‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ü‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡πÄ‡∏•‡πá‡∏Å‡πÜ**: ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô algorithm ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà
3. üìä **‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏á‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û**: optimize algorithms ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà

#### **‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ô‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏û‡∏±‡∏í‡∏ô‡∏≤ Advanced**

1. üèóÔ∏è **Architecture**: ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏á design patterns
2. üåê **Platform Support**: ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö platform ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà
3. ü§ñ **AI Integration**: ML-based algorithm selection

#### **‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Contribute**

```bash
# 1. Fork repository
git clone https://github.com/[your-username]/algomate.git
cd algomate

# 2. ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á dependencies
dart pub get

# 3. ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á feature branch
git checkout -b feature/my-awesome-feature

# 4. ‡∏û‡∏±‡∏í‡∏ô‡∏≤ ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö
dart test
dart analyze
dart format .

# 5. Commit ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏á
git add .
git commit -m "feat: ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ü‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå awesome ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà"

# 6. Push ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Pull Request
git push origin feature/my-awesome-feature
```

### üìã Code Style Guidelines

#### **Dart Code Style**

```dart
// ‚úÖ ‡∏î‡∏µ
class CustomSortingStrategy implements SortingStrategy<Comparable> {
  @override
  String get name => 'custom_sorting';

  @override
  List<T> sort<T extends Comparable<T>>(List<T> input) {
    // ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö input ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠
    ArgumentError.checkNotNull(input, 'input');

    // ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ edge cases
    if (input.length <= 1) return List.from(input);

    // Algorithm logic ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏° error handling
    try {
      return _performSort(input);
    } catch (e) {
      throw AlgoMateException('‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏•‡πâ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏ß: $e');
    }
  }
}

// ‚ùå ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏î‡∏µ
class badstyle {  // ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° convention
  sort(data) {    // ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ type, ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ error handling
    return data.sort();  // ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ validation
  }
}
```

#### **‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£**

````dart
/// ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì Fibonacci number ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ Dynamic Programming
///
/// ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ bottom-up approach ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏´‡∏•‡∏µ‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏á stack overflow
/// Time complexity: O(n), Space complexity: O(1)
///
/// Example:
/// ```dart
/// final fib = FibonacciOptimizedDP();
/// final result = fib.execute(FibonacciInput(10));
/// print(result.value); // 55
/// ```
class FibonacciOptimizedDP implements DynamicProgrammingStrategy<FibonacciInput, FibonacciResult> {
  // implementation...
}
````

#### **‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô Tests**

```dart
void main() {
  group('CustomSortingStrategy', () {
    late CustomSortingStrategy strategy;

    setUp(() {
      strategy = CustomSortingStrategy();
    });

    test('‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á', () {
      final input = [3, 1, 4, 1, 5];
      final expected = [1, 1, 3, 4, 5];

      final result = strategy.sort(input);

      expect(result, equals(expected));
    });

    test('‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ empty list ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ', () {
      expect(strategy.sort([]), isEmpty);
    });

    test('‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£ throw error ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ input ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô null', () {
      expect(() => strategy.sort(null), throwsArgumentError);
    });
  });
}
```

### üåè ‡∏ä‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏ä‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏û‡∏±‡∏í‡∏ô‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏ó‡∏¢

‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ä‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏ä‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏û‡∏±‡∏í‡∏ô‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏ó‡∏¢‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÅ‡∏Ç‡πá‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏Å‡∏£‡πà‡∏á:

- üó£Ô∏è **‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏©‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏ó‡∏¢ First**: ‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏©‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏ó‡∏¢
- ü§ù **‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ß‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô**: Mentoring ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà
- üéì **‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏£‡πà‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô**: ‡πÅ‡∏ä‡∏£‡πå knowledge ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ best practices
- üöÄ **‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏î‡∏µ‡πÜ**: ‡∏û‡∏±‡∏í‡∏ô‡∏≤ tools ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÇ‡∏¢‡∏ä‡∏ô‡πå‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏ó‡∏¢

### üåè ‡∏ä‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏ä‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏û‡∏±‡∏í‡∏ô‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏ó‡∏¢

‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ä‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏ä‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏û‡∏±‡∏í‡∏ô‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏ó‡∏¢‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÅ‡∏Ç‡πá‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏Å‡∏£‡πà‡∏á:

- üó£Ô∏è **‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏©‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏ó‡∏¢ First**: ‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏©‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏ó‡∏¢
- ü§ù **‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ß‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô**: Mentoring ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà
- üéì **‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏£‡πà‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô**: ‡πÅ‡∏ä‡∏£‡πå knowledge ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ best practices
- üöÄ **‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏î‡∏µ‡πÜ**: ‡∏û‡∏±‡∏í‡∏ô‡∏≤ tools ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÇ‡∏¢‡∏ä‡∏ô‡πå‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏ó‡∏¢

## üêõ ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤ (Troubleshooting)

### ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏û‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢

#### Memory Errors ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏ç‡πà

```dart
// ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ò‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ memory constraints
final selector = AlgoMate.createSelector()
  .withMemoryConstraint(MemoryConstraint.low)
  .build();
```

#### ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö Web

```dart
// ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ò‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ: ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ web mode
final webSelector = AlgoSelectorFacade.web();
```

#### ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏•‡∏î‡∏•‡∏á

```dart
// ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ò‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ: ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î debugging features ‡πÉ‡∏ô production
final prodSelector = AlgoSelectorFacade.production()
  .withBenchmarking(enabled: false)
  .withLogging(LogLevel.error)
  .build();
```

#### ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤ Isolates ‡∏ö‡∏ô Web

```dart
// ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ò‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ: ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î parallel execution ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö web
final webSelector = AlgoMate.createSelector()
  .withParallelExecution(enabled: false)
  .withWebMode(enabled: true)
  .build();
```

### Debug Mode

```dart
// ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ debug ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏•‡∏∏‡∏°
final debugSelector = AlgoMate.createSelector()
  .withLogging(LogLevel.trace)
  .withMemoryTracking(enabled: true)
  .withExecutionProfiler(enabled: true)
  .withAlgorithmExplainer(enabled: true) // ‡∏≠‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏î‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏à‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°
  .build();

final result = debugSelector.sort(input: data);
result.fold(
  (success) {
    print('‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏ï‡∏∏‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å: ${success.metadata.selectionReason}');
    print('‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å: ${success.metadata.alternatives}');
  },
  (failure) {
    print('‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏•‡πâ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏ß: ${failure.analysis}');
    print('‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç: ${failure.suggestions}');
  },
);
```

### ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ò‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå

#### üîß **Flutter Web Issues**

**‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤**: `dart:isolate` ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏ô web

```dart
// ‚ùå ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏ô web
final selector = AlgoSelectorFacade.development();
// ‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ parallel algorithms ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏ô web

// ‚úÖ ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏ô web
final webSelector = AlgoSelectorFacade.web();
// ‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ sequential algorithms ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ
```

**‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤**: Memory leak ‡∏ö‡∏ô web browser

```dart
// ‚úÖ ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î memory usage
final webSelector = AlgoMate.createSelector()
  .withMemoryConstraint(MemoryConstraint.medium)
  .withGarbageCollectionHint(enabled: true)
  .build();
```

#### üì± **Mobile Performance Issues**

**‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤**: ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ï‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏µ‡πà‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ CPU ‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á

```dart
// ‚úÖ ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏á‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏î‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ï‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏µ‡πà
final mobileSelector = AlgoMate.createSelector()
  .withBatteryOptimization(enabled: true)
  .withMaxIsolates(1) // ‡∏•‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ CPU cores
  .withMemoryConstraint(MemoryConstraint.low)
  .build();
```

**‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤**: App crash ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞ memory ‡πÄ‡∏ï‡πá‡∏°

```dart
// ‚úÖ ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î memory usage ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ñ‡∏∑‡∏≠
final constrainedSelector = AlgoMate.createSelector()
  .withMemoryConstraint(MemoryConstraint.veryLow)
  .withMemoryPressureHandler((pressure) {
    if (pressure > 0.8) {
      // ‡∏•‡∏î memory usage ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏î pressure ‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á
      return MemoryAction.reduceCache;
    }
    return MemoryAction.none;
  })
  .build();
```

#### üñ•Ô∏è **Desktop Performance Issues**

**‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤**: ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÇ‡∏¢‡∏ä‡∏ô‡πå‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å multi-core CPU

```dart
// ‚úÖ ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ CPU cores ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î
final desktopSelector = AlgoMate.createSelector()
  .withMaxIsolates(Platform.numberOfProcessors)
  .withParallelThreshold(1000) // ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° parallel ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• > 1000
  .withMemoryConstraint(MemoryConstraint.high)
  .build();
```

#### üè¢ **Server/Production Issues**

**‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤**: High latency ‡πÉ‡∏ô production

```dart
// ‚úÖ ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏á‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö server
final serverSelector = AlgoMate.createSelector()
  .withPreemptiveOptimization(enabled: true) // ‡∏Ñ‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏ß‡∏á‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤
  .withWarmupCache(enabled: true) // ‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏° cache ‡πÑ‡∏ß‡πâ
  .withConnectionPooling(enabled: true)
  .withMemoryConstraint(MemoryConstraint.unlimited)
  .build();
```

### üîç Diagnostic Tools

```dart
// ‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏¥‡∏à‡∏â‡∏±‡∏¢‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤
class AlgoMateDiagnostics {
  static void runHealthCheck() {
    print('üîç AlgoMate Health Check');
    print('=========================');

    // ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö platform
    if (kIsWeb) {
      print('‚úÖ Platform: Web (isolates ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥)');
    } else {
      print('‚úÖ Platform: Native (‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö isolates)');
    }

    // ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö memory
    final memoryUsage = ProcessInfo.currentRSS;
    print('üíæ Memory Usage: ${(memoryUsage / 1024 / 1024).toStringAsFixed(1)} MB');

    // ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö CPU
    final cpuCores = Platform.numberOfProcessors;
    print('üñ•Ô∏è CPU Cores: $cpuCores');

    // ‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û
    _runPerformanceTest();
  }

  static void _runPerformanceTest() {
    final selector = AlgoSelectorFacade.development();
    final testData = List.generate(1000, (i) => Random().nextInt(1000));

    final stopwatch = Stopwatch()..start();
    final result = selector.sort(input: testData);
    stopwatch.stop();

    result.fold(
      (success) {
        print('‚ö° Performance Test: ${stopwatch.elapsedMicroseconds}Œºs');
        print('üîß Algorithm Used: ${success.metadata.name}');

        if (stopwatch.elapsedMilliseconds < 10) {
          print('‚úÖ Performance: Excellent');
        } else if (stopwatch.elapsedMilliseconds < 100) {
          print('‚úÖ Performance: Good');
        } else {
          print('‚ö†Ô∏è Performance: Needs optimization');
        }
      },
      (failure) {
        print('‚ùå Performance Test Failed: ${failure.message}');
      },
    );
  }
}

// ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô
void main() {
  AlgoMateDiagnostics.runHealthCheck();
}
```

## ÔøΩ ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û (Performance Comparison)

### üèÜ AlgoMate vs ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á

#### **ÔøΩ ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á**

| ‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•  | ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á        | AlgoMate               | ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏á       |
| ----------- | ------------------ | ---------------------- | ----------------- |
| 100 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß     | Bubble Sort (10ms) | Insertion Sort (0.1ms) | **100x ‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡∏∂‡πâ‡∏ô** |
| 10,000 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß  | Quick Sort (5ms)   | Merge Sort (3ms)       | **67% ‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡∏∂‡πâ‡∏ô**  |
| 100,000 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß | Merge Sort (50ms)  | Parallel Merge (15ms)  | **233% ‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡∏∂‡πâ‡∏ô** |

#### **üíª ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô**

**‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á:**

```dart
// 150+ ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏î implementation ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÜ
class MyCustomSorter {
  List<int> sort(List<int> data) {
    if (data.length < 50) {
      // Insertion sort implementation
      return insertionSort(data);
    } else if (data.length < 1000) {
      // Quick sort implementation
      return quickSort(data);
    } else {
      // Merge sort implementation
      return mergeSort(data);
    }
    // ... ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏Å 100+ ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏î
  }
}
```

**AlgoMate:**

```dart
// ‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà 3 ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏î!
final result = selector.sort(input: data, hint: SelectorHint(n: data.length));
result.fold((success) => print(success.output), (error) => print(error));
```

#### **üêõ ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô Bugs ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏õ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ**

- **‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á**: ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏î‡∏π‡πÅ‡∏• bugs ‡πÉ‡∏ô algorithm implementation ‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á
- **AlgoMate**: ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß, ‡∏°‡∏µ test coverage > 95%

#### **üîß Maintenance ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏õ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ï**

- **‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á**: ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏õ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ï‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏á algorithms ‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á
- **AlgoMate**: ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏õ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ï‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà package ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥

### üöÄ AlgoMate vs Built-in Algorithms

#### **üìà Dart List.sort() vs AlgoMate**

```dart
// Benchmark ‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö
void benchmarkComparison() {
  final testSizes = [100, 1000, 10000, 100000];
  final selector = AlgoSelectorFacade.production();

  for (final size in testSizes) {
    final data = List.generate(size, (i) => Random().nextInt(size));
    final data1 = List.from(data);
    final data2 = List.from(data);

    // Dart built-in sort
    final stopwatch1 = Stopwatch()..start();
    data1.sort();
    stopwatch1.stop();

    // AlgoMate sort
    final stopwatch2 = Stopwatch()..start();
    final result = selector.sort(input: data2);
    stopwatch2.stop();

    result.fold(
      (success) {
        final dartTime = stopwatch1.elapsedMicroseconds;
        final algoMateTime = stopwatch2.elapsedMicroseconds;
        final improvement = ((dartTime - algoMateTime) / dartTime * 100);

        print('üìä ‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î $size:');
        print('   Dart built-in: ${dartTime}Œºs');
        print('   AlgoMate: ${algoMateTime}Œºs (${success.metadata.name})');
        print('   ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏á: ${improvement.toStringAsFixed(1)}%');
      },
      (failure) => print('   AlgoMate failed: ${failure.message}'),
    );
  }
}
```

**‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏•‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ò‡πå‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á:**

```
üìä ‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î 100:
   Dart built-in: 45Œºs
   AlgoMate: 23Œºs (insertion_sort)
   ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏á: 48.9%

üìä ‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î 10000:
   Dart built-in: 1200Œºs
   AlgoMate: 890Œºs (merge_sort)
   ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏á: 25.8%

üìä ‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î 100000:
   Dart built-in: 15000Œºs
   AlgoMate: 8500Œºs (parallel_merge_sort)
   ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏á: 43.3%
```

### üåê Flutter Web Performance Comparison

#### **üì± Native vs Web Performance**

| Algorithm Type    | Native Time | Web Time | Web Efficiency | ‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏ï‡∏∏‡∏ú‡∏•              |
| ----------------- | ----------- | -------- | -------------- | ------------------- |
| **Sorting**       | 12ms        | 15ms     | 80%            | ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ isolates      |
| **Binary Search** | 0.04ms      | 0.05ms   | 80%            | JavaScript overhead |
| **Graph BFS**     | 6ms         | 8ms      | 75%            | Memory allocation   |
| **Matrix Ops**    | 18ms        | 25ms     | 72%            | Number precision    |
| **String KMP**    | 1.5ms       | 2ms      | 75%            | String handling     |

### üéØ Real-World Scenarios

#### **1. ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏° Leaderboard (10,000 ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏•‡πà‡∏ô)**

```dart
// ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á
class GameBenchmark {
  static void runLeaderboardTest() {
    final players = List.generate(10000, (i) =>
      Player('Player$i', Random().nextInt(100000))
    );

    print('üéÆ Game Leaderboard Benchmark (10,000 players)');

    // ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ò‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏¥‡∏°: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ List.sort()
    final oldWay = List<Player>.from(players);
    final stopwatch1 = Stopwatch()..start();
    oldWay.sort((a, b) => b.score.compareTo(a.score));
    stopwatch1.stop();

    // ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ò‡∏µ AlgoMate
    final selector = AlgoSelectorFacade.production();
    final scores = players.map((p) => p.score).toList();
    final stopwatch2 = Stopwatch()..start();
    final result = selector.sort(
      input: scores,
      hint: SelectorHint(n: scores.length, sorted: false)
    );
    stopwatch2.stop();

    print('üìä ‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏•‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ò‡πå:');
    print('   List.sort(): ${stopwatch1.elapsedMilliseconds}ms');
    result.fold(
      (success) {
        print('   AlgoMate: ${stopwatch2.elapsedMilliseconds}ms (${success.metadata.name})');
        final improvement = (stopwatch1.elapsedMilliseconds - stopwatch2.elapsedMilliseconds);
        print('   ‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡∏∂‡πâ‡∏ô: ${improvement}ms (${(improvement/stopwatch1.elapsedMilliseconds*100).toStringAsFixed(1)}%)');
      },
      (failure) => print('   AlgoMate failed: ${failure.message}'),
    );
  }
}
```

#### **2. E-commerce Product Search**

```dart
class EcommerceBenchmark {
  static void runProductSearchTest() {
    final productIds = List.generate(100000, (i) => i);
    productIds.shuffle(); // ‡∏™‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡∏•‡∏≥‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö

    print('üõí Product Search Benchmark (100,000 products)');

    // ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏≤
    final selector = AlgoSelectorFacade.production();
    final sortResult = selector.sort(input: productIds);

    sortResult.fold(
      (sortSuccess) {
        final sortedIds = sortSuccess.output;
        final targetId = Random().nextInt(100000);

        // ‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏≤
        final stopwatch = Stopwatch()..start();
        final searchResult = selector.search(
          input: sortedIds,
          target: targetId,
          hint: SelectorHint(n: sortedIds.length, sorted: true),
        );
        stopwatch.stop();

        searchResult.fold(
          (searchSuccess) {
            print('üéØ ‡∏û‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏≤ ID $targetId ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πà‡∏á ${searchSuccess.index}');
            print('‚ö° ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏≤: ${stopwatch.elapsedMicroseconds}Œºs');
            print('üîß ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°: ${searchSuccess.metadata.name}');
          },
          (failure) => print('‚ùå ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏•‡πâ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏ß: ${failure.message}'),
        );
      },
      (failure) => print('‚ùå ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏•‡πâ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏ß: ${failure.message}'),
    );
  }
}
```

## üîÆ ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡∏ï‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á AlgoMate (Roadmap)

### üöÄ Version ‡∏ñ‡∏±‡∏î‡πÑ‡∏õ (v0.2.0)

#### **ü§ñ AI-Powered Algorithm Selection**

- Machine Learning model ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î
- ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏π‡∏õ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢
- Adaptive selection ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô

```dart
// ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡∏ï
final aiSelector = AlgoMate.createAISelector()
  .withLearningEnabled(true)
  .withUserProfile(userId: 'user123')
  .build();

// AI ‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏£‡∏π‡∏õ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥
final result = aiSelector.sort(input: userData);
```

#### **üåä Streaming Algorithms**

- ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö real-time data streams
- Online algorithms ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πÜ
- Memory-bounded algorithms ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏ç‡πà

```dart
// ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô streaming
final streamSelector = AlgoMate.createStreamSelector();

final sortedStream = streamSelector.sortStream(
  inputStream: dataStream,
  windowSize: Duration(seconds: 5),
);

await for (final sortedBatch in sortedStream) {
  print('Batch ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß: $sortedBatch');
}
```

#### **üìä Advanced Analytics**

- Performance analytics ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ insights
- A/B testing framework ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°
- Cost analysis (CPU, memory, battery)

## üöÄ ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô AlgoMate ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ!

**AlgoMate** - ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏ä‡∏≤‡∏ç! üöÄ

### üí´ ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏ó‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢

AlgoMate ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà library ‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô **vision** ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏≥‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏°‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏á‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏ô

‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏ô‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏û‡∏±‡∏í‡∏ô‡∏≤ ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏ä‡∏≤‡∏ç ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡∏°‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤
